Download

  • SnpEff & SnpSift: Download here the latest version of the core program.
  • Databases for SnpEff: The easiest way to download a SnpEff database is to use the 'download' command (see list of available databases below, or in the snpEff.config file). E.g. to downlaod GRCh37.68, just run: 
    java -jar snpEff.jar download GRCh37.68
  • Old versions: Old SnpEff, SnpSift and database versions can be found here.

Instruccions: Download SnpEff

  • Step 1: Download the core program here.
  • Step 2: Download the database/s you want to use. You can
    • Download manualy by clicking the link below, or
    • Use the 'download' command (see list of available databases below). E.g. to downlaod GRCh37.68, just run: 
      java -jar snpEff.jar download GRCh37.68
